 3974  Today, I've *officially* started working on two of language oriented projects which were brewing in my mind for a while. I introduce you to \n[taal-clj](https://github.com/abhi18av/taal-clj), which is a language learning tool I'm building and [kotoba-clj](https://github.com/abhi18av/kotoba-clj) the purpose of which is to 
 3975  explore the computational generation of langauges i.e. a tool for Constructed Languages.

 7951  cat << EOF > fibonacci.go\npackage main\n\nimport (\n"fmt"\n"math/big"\n)\n\nfunc main() {\n\t// Initialize two big ints with the first two numbers in the sequence.\n\ta := big.NewInt(0)\n\tb := big.NewInt(1)\n\n\t// Initialize limit as 10^99, the smallest integer with 100 digits.\n\tvar limit big.Int\n\tlimit.Exp(big.NewInt(10), big.NewInt(99), nil)\n\n\t// Loop while a is smaller than 1e100.\n\tfor a.Cmp(&limit) < 0 {\n\t\t// Compute the next Fibonacci number, storing it in a.\n\t\ta.Add(a, b)\n\t\t// Swap a and b so that b is the next number in the sequence.\n\t\ta, b = b, a\n\t}\n\tfmt.Println(a) // 100-digit Fibonacci number\n\n\t// Test a for primality.\n\t// (ProbablyPrimes' argument sets the number of Miller-Rabin\n// rounds to be performed. 20 is a good value.)\nfmt.Println(a.ProbablyPrime(20))\n\n}\n\n
